MuseScore peut exporter en PDF, PNG et d'autres formats graphiques mais aussi en WAV et d'autres formats audio.","ProductFamilyName":"Apps","Schema":"Card;1"}],"Title":"Les plus populaires","HasThirdPartyIAPs":false,"AlgoName":"RECO-Algo-Version","AlgoValue":"Lists;mostPopular;;Apps;00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000003","TotalItems":932,"PageSize":200}}
